[38;2;255;255;255m⏺[39m [1mRoot Cause Analysis[22m

  The program crashes due to a [1mnull pointer dereference[22m in the [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m
  function at [38;2;177;185;249mdemo-buggy.c:26[39m.

  [1mLocation of crash:[22m
  - Function: [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m at line 26 in demo-buggy.c
  - Specific line: [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[s->num_scores] = score;[39m

  [1mRoot cause:[22m
  The [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m field in the Student struct is a null pointer
  ([38;2;177;185;249m0x0000000000000000[39m), but the code attempts to write to it without first
  allocating memory. When the program tries to access [38;2;177;185;249ms->scores[0][39m (since
  [38;2;177;185;249mnum_scores=0[39m), it attempts to write to memory address 0x0, which causes a
   segmentation fault (EXC_BAD_ACCESS).

  [1mVariable examination:[22m
  - Student struct is valid (address: [38;2;177;185;249m0x0000000131e05580[39m)
  - Student name: "Alice" (valid)
  - Student age: 20 (valid)
  - [1mscores pointer: 0x0 (NULL) - This is the problem[22m
  - num_scores: 0 (valid)

  [1mCall stack:[22m
  1. [38;2;177;185;249mmain()[39m calls [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m at demo-buggy.c:56
  2. [38;2;177;185;249madd_score()[39m crashes when accessing the null [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m pointer

  The bug is that the [38;2;177;185;249mscores[39m array was never allocated memory before
  attempting to use it. The program needs to allocate memory for the scores
   array (e.g., using [38;2;177;185;249mmalloc()[39m) before storing any scores.
